<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:0pt;;text-indent:0pt;;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement</p></td>

<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.14%;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The information set forth in Item 8.01 of this Current Report on Form&#160;8-K&#160;under the headings &#8220;Supplemental Indenture Relating to Convertible Senior Notes,&#8221; &#8220;Additional Note Hedge Transactions&#8221; and &#8220;Additional Warrant Transactions&#8221; is incorporated by reference into this Item 1.01.</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:18pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>

<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:0pt;;text-indent:0pt;;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Creation of a Direct Financial Obligation or an Obligation under an&#160;Off-Balance&#160;Sheet Arrangement of a Registrant</p></td>

<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:18pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">

<td valign="top"  BGCOLOR="#FFFFFF" style="width:auto;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:0pt;;text-indent:0pt;;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Unregistered Sales of Equity Securities</p></td>
</tr>
</table></div>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.14%;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The information set forth in Item 8.01 of this Current Report on Form&#160;8-K&#160;under the heading &#8220;Additional Warrant Transactions&#8221; is incorporated by reference into this Item 3.02.</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:18pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top"  BGCOLOR="#FFFFFF" style="width:12%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:0pt;;text-indent:0pt;;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Item&#160;8.01</p></td>
<td valign="top"  BGCOLOR="#FFFFFF" style="width:auto;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:0pt;;text-indent:0pt;;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Other Events</p></td>
</tr>
</table></div>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.14%;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">On May 7, 2019, Tesla, Inc. (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Company</font>&#8221;) closed its previously announced underwritten public offerings of (1) 3,549,381 shares of common stock of the Company, par value $0.001 per share (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Common Stock</font>&#8221;), which includes 462,962 shares sold pursuant to the underwriters&#8217; (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Underwriters</font>&#8221;) option to purchase additional shares, which was exercised in full on May 3, 2019; and (2) $1.84 billion aggregate principal amount of the Company&#8217;s 2.00% Convertible Senior Notes due May 15, 2024 (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Notes</font>&#8221;), which includes $240.0 million aggregate principal amount of Notes sold pursuant to the Underwriters&#8217; option to purchase additional Notes (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Option Notes</font>&#8221;), which was exercised in full on May 3, 2019, in each case pursuant to a Registration Statement on Form&#160;S-3 (File&#160;No.&#160;333-231168) (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Registration Statement</font>&#8221;) and accompanying prospectus, together with the related prospectus supplements for the underwritten public offerings of the Common Stock and the Notes, filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission.</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.14%;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">In connection with these offerings, the legal opinion as to the legality of the Common Stock and the Notes sold is being filed as Exhibit 5.1 to this Current Report on Form&#160;8-K&#160;and is incorporated herein and into the Registration Statement by reference.</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:18pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Supplemental Indenture Relating to Convertible Senior Notes</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.14%;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">On May 7, 2019, the Company entered into a Fifth Supplemental Indenture relating to the issuance by the Company of the Notes (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;) supplementing the Indenture, dated May&#160;22, 2013 (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Base Indenture</font>,&#8221; and together with the Supplemental Indenture, the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Indenture</font>&#8221;), by and between the Company and U.S. Bank National Association , as trustee (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Trustee</font>&#8221;). The Notes will bear interest at a rate of 2.00%&#160;per year, payable semi-annually in arrears on May&#160;15 and November&#160;15 of each year, commencing November&#160;15, 2019. The Notes will mature on May&#160;15, 2024, unless, in each case, earlier repurchased by the Company or converted pursuant to their respective terms.</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.14%;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The initial conversion rate of the Notes is 3.2276 shares of Common Stock per $1,000 principal amount of the Notes (which is equivalent to an initial conversion price of approximately $309.83 per share). The conversion rate for the Notes will be subject to adjustment upon the occurrence of certain specified events but will not be adjusted for accrued and unpaid interest. In addition, upon the occurrence of a &#8220;make-whole fundamental change&#8221; (as defined in the Supplemental Indenture), the Company will, in certain circumstances, increase the conversion rate by a number of additional shares for a holder that elects to convert the Notes in connection with such make-whole fundamental change.</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.14%;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU2"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Prior to the close of business on the business day immediately preceding </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">February&#160;15, 2024</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">, the Notes will be convertible o</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">nly under the following circumstances: (1)&#160;during any calendar quarter commencing after </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">September&#160;30, 2019</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> (and only during such calendar quarter), if the last reported sale price of the Common Stock for at least 20 trading days (whether or not consecutive</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">) during a period of 30 consecutive trading days ending on the last trading day of the immediately preceding calendar quarter is greater than or equal to 130% of the conversion price on each trading day; (2)&#160;during the five business day period after any fi</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">ve consecutive trading day period in which the trading price per $1,000 principal amount of the Notes for each trading day of such period was less than 98% of the product of the last reported sale price of Common Stock and the conversion rate on each such </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">trading day; or (3)&#160;upon the occurrence of specified corporate events. On or after </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">February 15, 2024</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">, until the close of business on the second scheduled trading day immediately preceding the maturity date, holders may convert the Notes at any time. Upon c</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">onversion, the Notes will be settled in cash, shares of Common Stock or a combination thereof, at the Company&#8217;s election.</font></p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.14%;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The Company may not redeem the Notes prior to the maturity date; however, upon the occurrence of a fundamental change (as defined in the Supplemental Indenture), holders may require the Company to purchase all or a portion of the Notes for cash at a price equal to 100% of the principal amount of the Notes to be purchased plus any accrued and unpaid interest to, but excluding, the fundamental change purchase date.</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.14%;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The Notes will be the Company&#8217;s senior unsecured obligations and will rank senior in right of payment to any of the Company&#8217;s indebtedness that is expressly subordinated in right of payment to the Notes, will rank equally in right of payment with any of the Company&#8217;s unsecured indebtedness that is not so subordinated, including the Company&#8217;s outstanding 1.25% Convertible Senior Notes due 2021, 2.375% Convertible Senior Notes due 2022, and 5.30% Senior Notes due 2025, and will be effectively junior in right of payment to any of the Company&#8217;s secured indebtedness to the extent of the value of the assets securing such indebtedness and will be structurally subordinated to all indebtedness and other liabilities of the Company&#8217;s subsidiaries.</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.14%;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Each of the following events is considered an &#8220;event of default&#8221; with respect to the Notes, which may result in the acceleration of the maturity of the Notes:</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>

<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.14%;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">If an event of default occurs with respect to the Notes, and is continuing (other than an event of default described in clause (8)&#160;above with respect to the Company (and not with respect to a &#8220;significant subsidiary&#8221;)), the Trustee by notice to the Company, or the holders of at least 25% in principal amount of the outstanding Notes, by notice to the Company and the Trustee, may declare 100% of the principal of and accrued and unpaid interest on all the Notes to be due and payable; upon such a declaration, such principal and any accrued and unpaid interest will be due and payable immediately, subject to certain limitations in the case of an event of default relating to certain failures by the Company to make certain filings required by it to be made with the Trustee or the Securities and Exchange Commission pursuant to the Trust Indenture Act of 1939, as amended, or the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, respectively. Upon an event of default described in clause (8) above with respect to the Company, 100% of the aggregate principal amount and accrued and unpaid interest on the Notes will automatically be due and payable immediately.</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.14%;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The summary of the foregoing transactions is qualified in its entirety by reference to the text of the Base Indenture, the Supplemental Indenture, and the Form of 2.00% Convertible Senior Note due May&#160;15, 2024 included in the Supplemental Indenture (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Global Note</font>&#8221;), which are filed as Exhibits 4.1, 4.2 and 4.3, respectively, with this Current Report on Form&#160;8-K&#160;and are incorporated herein and into the Registration Statement by reference.</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:18pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Additional Note Hedge Transactions</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:7.14%;">On May 3, 2019, in connection with the exercise of the Underwriters&#8217; option to purchase the Option Notes, the Company entered into additional note hedge transactions (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Additional Note Hedge Transactions</font>&#8221;) with each of Soci&#233;t&#233; G&#233;n&#233;rale, Wells Fargo Bank, National Association, Goldman Sachs &amp; Co. LLC, and Credit Suisse Capital LLC, with Credit Suisse Securities (USA) LLC as agent, or their respective affiliates (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Hedge Counterparties</font>&#8221;)<font style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;">, pursuant to call option confirmations in substantially the form of Exhibit 10.1 to this Current Report on Form&#160;8-K,&#160;which is incorporated herein by reference. The Additional Note Hedge Transactions are expected generally to reduce the potential dilution to the Common Stock, and/or offset potential cash payments in excess of the principal amount upon any conversion of the Option Notes in the event that the market value per share of the Common Stock, as measured under the terms of the Additional Note Hedge Transactions, is greater than the strike prices of the Additional Note Hedge Transactions (which correspond to the initial conversion price of the Notes and are subject to certain adjustments substantially similar to those contained in the Notes). On May 7, 2019, at the closing of the offering of the Notes, the Company paid an aggregate amount of approximately $475.8 million to the Hedge Counterparties for note hedge transactions in connection with the Notes, including approximately $62.1 million for the Additional Note Hedge Transactions</font>.</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-top:18pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Additional Warrant Transactions</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:18pt;margin-top:6pt;text-indent:7.14%;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU5"></a>On May 3, 2019, in connection with the exercise of the Underwriters&#8217; option to purchase the Option Notes, the Company entered into additional warrant confirmations with each of the Hedge Counterparties in substantially the form of Exhibit 10.2 to this Current Report on Form 8-K, which is incorporated herein by reference, pursuant to which the Company issued certain warrants (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Additional Warrants</font>&#8221;). The Additional Warrants allow the Hedge Counterparties to acquire, subject to anti-dilution adjustments, up to approximately 1.5 million shares of Common Stock at a strike price of $607.50 per share, which is also subject to adjustment. The Additional Warrants would separately have a dilutive effect to the extent that the market value per share of the </p>

<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:18pt;margin-top:6pt;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Common Stock exceeds the strike p</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">rice of the Additional Warrants </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">unless, subj</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">ect to the terms of the warra</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">nt </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">confirmations, the Company elects to cash settle the </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Additional </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Warrants. The </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Additional Warrants were issued </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">pursuant to the exemption provided by Section 4(a)(2) of the Securities Act of 1933, as ame</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">nded. The Additional </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Warrants are separate transacti</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">ons, entered into by the Company with the Hedge C</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">ounterparties, and are not part </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">of the terms of the Option Notes. Holders of the Option Notes will not have</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> any rights with respect to the </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Additional Warrants. On </font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">May 7, 2019</font><font <td valign="top"  style="width:76.44%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:0pt;;text-indent:0pt;;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Form of Note</p></td>
<td valign="bottom"  style="width:7.4%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:0pt;;text-indent:0pt;;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">A-1</p></td>

<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">iii</a></p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU3"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">FIFTH SUPPLEMENTAL INDENTURE</font><font style="font-weight:bold;"> &#160;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">dated as of May 7, 2019 (this &#8220;</font><font style="font-weight:bold;">Supplemental Indenture</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8221;) between Tesla, Inc. (f/k/a/ Tesla Motors, Inc.), a Delaware corporation, as issuer (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-weight:bold;">Company</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8221;, as more fully set forth in Section&#160;1.01) and U.S. Bank National Association, a national banking association, as trustee (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-weight:bold;">Trustee</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8221;, as more fully set forth in Section&#160;1.01), supplementing the Indenture, dated as of May 22, 2013, between the Company and the Trustee (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-weight:bold;">Base Indenture</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8221; and the Base Indenture, as amended and supplemented by this Supplemental Indenture, and as it may be further amended or supplemented from time to time with respect to the Notes, the &#8220;</font><font style="font-weight:bold;">Indenture</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8221;).</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">W I T N E S S E T H:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">WHEREAS, the Company executed and delivered the Base Indenture to the Trustee to provide, among other things, for the issuance, from time to time, of the Company&#8217;s Securities, in an unlimited aggregate principal amount, in one or more series to be established by the Company under, and authenticated and delivered as provided in, the Base Indenture;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">WHEREAS, Sections 2.01 and 2.02 of the Base Indenture provide for the Company to issue Securities thereunder in the form and on the terms set forth in one or more Board Resolutions, indentures supplemental thereto or Officers&#8217; Certificates;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">WHEREAS, for its lawful corporate purposes, the Company has duly authorized the issuance of a single series of Securities designated as its 2.00% Convertible Senior Notes due 2024 (the &#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Notes</font>&#8221; and each $1,000 principal amount thereof, unless the context otherwise requires, a &#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Note</font>&#8221;), initially in an aggregate principal amount not to exceed <font style="color:#000000;">$1,840,000,000</font>, and in order to provide the terms and conditions upon which the Notes are to be authenticated, issued and delivered, the Company has duly authorized the execution and delivery of this Supplemental Indenture;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">WHEREAS, the Form&#160;of Note, the Form&#160;of Notice of Conversion, the Form&#160;of Fundamental Change Purchase Notice and the Form&#160;of Assignment and Transfer to be borne by the Notes are to be substantially in the forms hereinafter provided;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">WHEREAS, the conditions set forth in the Base Indenture for the execution and delivery of this Supplemental Indenture have been complied with; and</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">WHEREAS, all acts and things necessary to make the Notes, when executed by the Company and authenticated and delivered by the Trustee or a duly authorized authenticating agent, as in this Supplemental Indenture provided, the valid, binding and legal obligations of the Company, and this Supplemental Indenture a valid agreement according to its terms, have been done and performed, and the execution of this Supplemental Indenture and the issue hereunder of the Notes have in all respects been duly authorized.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.84%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">NOW, THEREFORE, THIS SUPPLEMENTAL INDENTURE WITNESSETH:</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.84%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU4"></a>That in order to declare the terms and conditions upon which the Notes are, and are to be, authenticated, issued and delivered, and in consideration of the premises and of the purchase and </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">1</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:7.69%;"><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font>&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">acceptance of the Notes by the Holders thereof, the Company covenants and agrees with the Trustee for the benefit of each other and for the equal and proportionate benefit of the respective Holders from time to time of the Notes (except as otherwise provided below), as follows:</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#010000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc356831190"></a><a name="_Toc356832094"></a><a name="_Toc477456653"></a><a name="_Toc7793042"></a>ARTICLE 1<font style="color:#000000;"><br /><a name="_Toc356831190"></a><a name="_Toc356832094"></a><a name="_Toc477456653"></a><a name="_Toc7793042"></a>DEFINITIONS</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc356831191"></a><a name="_Toc356832095"></a><a name="_Toc477456654"></a><a name="_Toc7793043"></a>Section 1.01<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-style:italic;">Definitions.</font>&#160; For all purposes of the Indenture, except as otherwise expressly provided or unless the context otherwise requires:</p>
<p style="margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font>the terms defined in this Article&#160;1 shall have the respective meanings assigned to them in this Article&#160;1 and include the plural as well as the singular and, to the extent applicable, supersede the definitions thereof in the Base Indenture;</p>
<p style="margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font>all words, terms and phrases defined in the Base Indenture (but not otherwise defined herein) shall have the same meanings as in the Base Indenture; and</p>
<p style="margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(c)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font>the words &#8220;herein,&#8221; &#8220;hereof&#8221; and &#8220;hereunder&#8221; and other words of similar import (i)&#160;when used with regard to any specified Article, Section&#160;or sub-division, refer to such Article, Section&#160;or sub-division of this Supplemental Indenture and (ii)&#160;otherwise, refer to the Indenture as a whole and not to any particular Article, Section&#160;or other subdivision.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Additional Interest</font>&#8221; means all amounts, if any, payable pursuant to Section&#160;5.04.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Additional Shares</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;9.03(a).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Additional Notes</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section 2.08(a).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Base Indenture</font>&#8221; has the meaning specified in the first paragraph of this Supplemental Indenture.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Bid Solicitation Agent</font>&#8221; means the Person appointed by the Company to solicit bids for the Trading Price of the Notes in accordance with Section&#160;9.01(b)(i).&#160; The Company shall initially act as the Bid Solicitation Agent.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Capital Stock</font>&#8221; means any and all shares, interests, participations, rights or other equivalents (however designated) of capital stock, including, without limitation, with respect to partnerships, partnership interests (whether general or limited) and any other interest or participation that confers on a person the right to receive a share of the profits and losses of, or distributions of assets of, such partnership. </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Cash Settlement</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;9.02(a).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Clause A Distribution</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;9.04(c).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Clause B Distribution</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;9.04(c).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Clause C Distribution</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;9.04(c).</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">2</a></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:7.69%;"><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font>&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU5"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">close of business</font>&#8221; means 5:00&#160;p.m., New York City time, on a Business Day.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Combination Settlement</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;9.02(a).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.76%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Common Equity</font>&#8221; of any Person means Capital Stock of such Person that are generally entitled (a)&#160;to vote in the election of directors of such Person or (b)&#160;if such Person is not a corporation, to vote or otherwise participate in the selection of the governing body, partners, managers or others that will control the management or policies of such Person, and in each case, not entitled to any preference in respect of dividends or amounts payable in the event of any voluntary or involuntary liquidation, dissolution or winding-up of such Person.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Common Stock</font>&#8221; means the common stock of the Company, par value $0.001 per share, at the date of this Supplemental Indenture, subject to Section&#160;9.07.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Company</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in the first paragraph of this Supplemental Indenture, and subject to the provisions of Article&#160;12 hereof, shall include its successors and assigns.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Conversion Agent</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;4.02.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Conversion Date</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;9.02(c).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Conversion Obligation</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;9.01(a).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Conversion Price</font>&#8221; means at any time, $1,000,<font style="font-style:italic;"> divided by</font> the Conversion Rate at such time.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Conversion Rate</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;9.01(a).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Conversion Settlement Amount</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;9.02(a)(3).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Daily Conversion Value</font>&#8221; means, for each of the 20 consecutive VWAP Trading Days during the Observation Period, 1/20th of the product of :</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.77%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;">&#160;the Conversion Rate on such VWAP Trading Day; and </font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.77%;text-indent:5.88%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.77%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;">&#160;the Daily VWAP on such VWAP Trading Day.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Daily Measurement Value</font>&#8221; means the Specified Dollar Amount <font style="font-style:italic;">divided by</font> 20.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">3</a></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:7.69%;"><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font>&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU6"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;</font><font style="font-weight:bold;">Daily Settlement Amount</font><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">,&#8221; for each of the 20 consecutive VWAP Trading Days during the applicable Observation Period, shall consist of:</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.88%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; cash equal to the lesser of (i) the Daily Measurement Value and (ii) the Daily Conversion Value; and</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.88%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.88%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; if the Daily Conversion Value on such VWAP Trading Day exceeds the Daily Measurement Value, a number of shares of Common Stock equal to (i) the difference between the Daily Conversion Value and the Daily Measurement Value, divided by (ii) the Daily VWAP on such VWAP Trading Day.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.88%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Daily VWAP</font>&#8221; means, for each of the 20 consecutive VWAP Trading Days during the applicable Observation Period, the per share volume-weighted average price as displayed under the heading &#8220;Bloomberg VWAP&#8221; on Bloomberg page&#160;&#8220;TSLA.Q &lt;EQUITY&gt; AQR&#8221; (or its equivalent successor if such page&#160;is not available) in respect of the period from the scheduled open of trading until the scheduled close of trading of the primary trading session on such VWAP Trading Day (or if such volume-weighted average price is unavailable, the market value of one share of Common Stock on such VWAP Trading Day reasonably determined, using a volume-weighted average method, by a nationally recognized independent investment banking firm retained for this purpose by the Company).&#160; The &#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Daily VWAP</font>&#8221; shall be determined without regard to after-hours trading or any other trading outside of the regular trading session trading hours.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Defaulted Amounts</font>&#8221; means any amounts on any Note (including, without limitation, the Fundamental Change Purchase Price, principal and interest) that are payable but are not paid or duly provided for when due.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Designated Institution</font><font style="color:#000000;">&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section 9.13(a).</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Distributed Property</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;9.04(c).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Effective Date</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;9.03(c), except that, as used in Section&#160;9.04, &#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Effective Date</font> &#8221; means the first date on which shares of the Common Stock trade on the Relevant Stock Exchange, regular way, reflecting the relevant share split or share combination, as applicable.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Event of Default</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;5.02, notwithstanding anything to the contrary in the Base Indenture.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Ex-Dividend Date</font>&#8221; means the first date on which the shares of Common Stock trade on the Relevant Stock Exchange, regular way, without the right to receive the issuance, dividend or distribution in question, from the Company or, if applicable, from the seller of Common Stock on the Relevant Stock Exchange (in the form of due bills or otherwise) as determined by the Relevant Stock Exchange.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Expiration Date</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;9.04(e).</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">4</a></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:7.69%;"><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font>&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU7"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Form&#160;of Assignment and Transfer</font>&#8221; shall mean the &#8220;Form&#160;of Assignment and Transfer&#8221; attached as Attachment 3 to the Form&#160;of Note attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;A.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Form&#160;of Fundamental Change Purchase Notice</font>&#8221; shall mean the &#8220;Form&#160;of Fundamental Change Purchase Notice&#8221; attached as Attachment 2 to the Form&#160;of Note attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;A.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Form&#160;of Notice of Conversion</font>&#8221; shall mean the &#8220;Form&#160;of Notice of Conversion&#8221; attached as Attachment 1 to the Form&#160;of Note attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;A.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">A &#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Fundamental Change</font>&#8221; shall be deemed to have occurred at the time after the Notes are originally issued if any of the following occurs:</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.88%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; a &#8220;person&#8221; or &#8220;group&#8221; within the meaning of Section&#160;13(d)&#160;of the Exchange Act, other than the Company, its wholly owned Subsidiaries or the employee benefit plans of the Company or its wholly owned Subsidiaries, files a Schedule TO or any schedule, form or report under the Exchange Act disclosing that such person or group has become the direct or indirect &#8220;beneficial owner,&#8221; as defined in Rule&#160;13d-3 under the Exchange Act, of the Company&#8217;s Common Equity representing more than 50% of the voting power of the Company&#8217;s Common Equity;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.88%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; the consummation of (1)&#160;except as set forth in clause (2) below, any recapitalization, reclassification or change of the Common Stock (other than changes resulting from a subdivision or combination) as a result of which the Common Stock would be converted into, or exchanged for, cash, securities or other property or assets; (2)&#160;any consolidation, merger, combination, statutory or binding share exchange or similar transaction involving the Company pursuant to which the Common Stock will be converted into cash, securities or other property or assets; or (3)&#160;any sale, conveyance, lease or other transfer or similar transaction in one transaction or a series of related transactions of all or substantially all of the consolidated assets of the Company and its Subsidiaries, taken as a whole, to any Person other than one or more of the Company&#8217;s Subsidiaries;<font style="font-style:italic;"> provided, however</font>, that neither (A) a transaction described in clause (1)&#160;or (2)&#160;in which the holders of all classes of the Company&#8217;s Common Equity immediately prior to such transaction own, directly or indirectly, more than 50% of all classes of Common Equity of the continuing or surviving corporation or transferee or the parent thereof immediately after such transaction in substantially the same proportions as such ownership immediately prior to such transaction nor (B) any merger of the Company solely for the purpose of changing its jurisdiction of incorporation that results in a reclassification, conversion or exchange of outstanding shares of Common Stock solely into shares of Common Equity of the surviving entity shall be a Fundamental Change pursuant to this clause (b);</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.88%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.88%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; the stockholders of the Company approve any plan or proposal for the liquidation or dissolution of the Company; or</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.88%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">5</a></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:7.69%;"><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font>&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.88%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU8"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; the Common Stock (or other common stock underlying the Notes) ceases to be listed or quoted on any of the NASDAQ Global Select Market, the NASDAQ Global Market or the New York Stock Exchange (or any of their respective successors);</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.88%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">provided<font style="font-style:normal;">,</font> however<font style="font-style:normal;">, that a transaction or transactions described in clause (a)&#160;or clause (b)&#160;above shall not constitute a Fundamental Change if at least 90% of the consideration received or to be received by holders of the Common Stock (excluding cash payments for fractional shares or pursuant to statutory appraisal rights) in connection with such transaction or transactions consists of shares of common stock or depositary receipts representing Common Equity interests, in each case, that are listed or quoted on any of the NASDAQ Global Select Market, the NASDAQ Global Market or the New York Stock Exchange (or any of their respective successors) or will be so listed or quoted when issued or exchanged in connection with such transaction or transactions (such securities, &#8220;</font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;">Publicly Traded Securities</font><font style="font-style:normal;">&#8221;) and, as a result of such transaction or transactions, the Notes become convertible into such Publicly Traded Securities, excluding cash payments for fractional shares or pursuant to statutory appraisal rights (subject to the provisions of Section&#160;9.02(a)). Any transaction or event that constitutes a Fundamental Change under both clause (a) and clause (b) without giving effect to the proviso in clause (b) above will be deemed to be solely a Fundamental Change under clause (b) of such definition (subject to the proviso to clause (b)).</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Fundamental Change Company Notice</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;10.01(c).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Fundamental Change Purchase Date</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;10.01(a).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Fundamental Change Purchase Notice</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;10.01(b)(i).</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Fundamental Change Purchase Price</font>&#8221; shall have the meaning specified in Section&#160;10.01(a).</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Global Note</font>&#8221; means a Note in the form of a Global Security.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Indenture</font>&#8221; has the meaning specified in the first paragraph of this Supplemental Indenture.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Interest Payment Date</font>&#8221; means each May 15 and November 15 of each year, beginning on November 15, 2019.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU9"></a>&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Last Reported Sale Price</font>&#8221; of the Common Stock on any date means the closing sale price per share (or if no closing sale price is reported, the average of the bid and ask prices or, if more than one in either case, the average of the average bid and the average ask prices) on that date as reported in composite transactions for the Relevant Stock Exchange.&#160; If the Common Stock is not listed, quoted or traded on any U.S. securities exchange or any other market, the &#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Last Reported Sale Price</font>&#8221; shall be the average of the mid-point of the last bid and ask prices </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">6</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:7.69%;"><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font>&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">for the Common Stock on the relevant date from each of at least three nationally recognized independent investment banking firms selected by the Company for this purpose.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Make-Whole Fundamental Change</font>&#8221; means any transaction or event that constitutes a Fundamental Change as set forth in clause (a), (b)&#160;or (d)&#160;of the definition thereof, after giving effect to any exceptions to or exclusions from such definition, but without regard to the<font style="font-style:italic;"> proviso</font> in clause (b)&#160;of the definition thereof.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="font-weight:bold;">Market Disruption Event</font>&#8221; means:</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:5.88%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.77%;text-indent:5.88%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(i)<font style="margin-left:36pt;">a failure by the Relevant Stock Exchange to open for trading during its regular trading session; or </font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:5.77%;text-indent:5.88%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
